add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #Afghanistan
	id = annex.1
	title = annex.1.t
	desc = annex.1.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AFG
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = AFG_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = AFG
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.1.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AFG
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			AFG = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = AFG
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.1.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = AFG_annex
	}
}
country_event = { #Alaska
	id = annex.2
	title = annex.2.t
	desc = annex.2.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.2.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ALA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			ALA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = ALA
	}

	option = { #give to american ally/puppet
		name = annex.2.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ALA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_country = { #this should only be one possible country
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.2.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = ALA_annex
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Algeria
	id = annex.5
	title = annex.5.t
	desc = annex.5.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.5.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				UAR = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ALG
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			ALG = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = ALG
	}

	option = { #give to UAR
		name = annex.5.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = UAR
			}
			UAR = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ALG
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			UAR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.5.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = ALG_annex
	}
}
country_event = { #Amalfi
	id = annex.6
	title = annex.6.t
	desc = annex.6.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = AMA
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = AMA_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = AMA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AMA
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = AMA_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = AMA
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.6.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		AMA = {
			transfer_state = 946
		}
		puppet = AMA
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.6.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = AMA_annex
	}
}

country_event = { #Australia
	id = annex.13
	title = annex.13.t
	desc = annex.13.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.13.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AST
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			AST = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = AST
	}

	option = { #balkanize
		name = annex.13.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		set_country_flag = AST_balkanize
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.13.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = AST_annex
	}
}

country_event = { #Balochistan
	id = annex.18
	title = annex.18.t
	desc = annex.18.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.18.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BAL
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			BAL = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = BAL
	}

	option = { #give to allies
		name = annex.18.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = PER
				tag = PAK
			}
			OR = {
				PER = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				PAK = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PER = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			PER = {
				transfer_state = 410
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				PAK = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			PAK = {
				transfer_state = 444
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.18.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = BAL_annex
	}
}
country_event = { #Bangladesh
	id = annex.19
	title = annex.19.t
	desc = annex.19.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

			base = 100
		}

					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}

				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = BNG
	}

			base = 10
		}

				tag = RAJ
			}

					is_puppet_of = ROOT

				}
			}
		}

				is_core_of = BNG

				}
			}
			RAJ = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	#	}
	#}

			base = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = BGL
			}

				OR = {

country_event = { #Brazil
	id = annex.31
	title = annex.31.t
	desc = annex.31.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.31.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BRA
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			BRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = BRA
	}

	option = { #balkanize
		name = annex.31.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 502
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BRA
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = SUL
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			BRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = BRA
		set_country_flag = BRA_balkanize
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.31.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = BRA_annex
	}
}
country_event = { #British Raj (India)
	id = annex.33
	title = annex.33.t
	desc = annex.33.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = RAJ
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = RAJ_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = RAJ
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = RAJ
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = RAJ_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = RAJ
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.33.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = RAJ
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			RAJ = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = RAJ
		hidden_effect = {
			RAJ = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #balkanize completely
		name = annex.33.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		set_country_flag = RAJ_balkanize
	}

	option = { #state by state balkanize
		name = annex.33.o3
		RAJ = {
			transfer_state = 439
			transfer_state = 951
			transfer_state = 952
		}
		puppet = RAJ
		hidden_effect = {
			RAJ = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = RAJ_balkanize
	}

	#option = { #give to PAK
	#	name = annex.33.o4
	#	ai_chance = {
	#		base = 100
	#	}
	#}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.33.o5
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = RAJ_annex
	}
}

country_event = { #Canada
	id = annex.41
	title = annex.41.t
	desc = annex.41.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = CAN
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = CAN_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = CAN
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CAN
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = CAN_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = CAN
			}
			every_state = {
				remove_claim_by = CAN
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.41.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAN
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			}
		}
		puppet = CAN
	}

	option = { #balkanize
		name = annex.41.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 466
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAN				
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = QUE
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CAN_balkanize
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			}
		}
		puppet = CAN
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.41.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = CAN_annex
	}
}
country_event = { #Cascadia
	id = annex.42
	title = annex.42.t
	desc = annex.42.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = CSD
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = CSD_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = CSD
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CSD
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = CSD_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = CSD
			}
			every_state = {
				remove_claim_by = CSD
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.42.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CSD
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					state = 890
				}
			}
			CSD = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			CSD = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			}
		}
		puppet = CSD
	}

	option = { #give to american ally/puppet
		name = annex.42.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CSD
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_country = { #this should only be one possible country
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.42.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = CSD_annex
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Egypt
	id = annex.67
	title = annex.67.t
	desc = annex.67.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = EGY
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = EGY_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = EGY
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = EGY
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = EGY_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = EGY
			}
			every_state = {
				remove_claim_by = EGY
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.67.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					tag = SYR
					has_global_flag = sharaf_has_invaded_syria
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = EGY
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			EGY = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = EGY
		hidden_effect = {
			EGY = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #SYR option
		name = annex.67.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			tag = SYR
			has_global_flag = sharaf_has_invaded_syria
		}

		country_event = syria.1
	}
	
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.67.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = EGY_annex
	}

					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					is_in_array = {
						array = ERI_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
			}
			ETH = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = {
					array = ERI_starting_cores
					value = THIS
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = ETH
		}
		puppet = ETH
		ETH = {
			load_focus_tree = generic_focus
		}
		set_country_flag = ETH_balkanize
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.71.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = ETH_annex
	}

					}
				}

			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = GRL

					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = moderate_socialist
				has_government = national_conservative
				has_government = new_democrat
			}
		}

			}

		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GRL = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			}

country_event = { #Italy
	id = annex.103
	title = annex.103.t
	desc = annex.103.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ITA
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = ITA_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ITA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ITA
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = ITA_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = ITA
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.103.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ITA
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 39 #South Tyrol
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = ITA
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #balkanize (confederation)
		name = annex.103.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ITA
				NOT = {
					state = 39 #South Tyrol
					is_in_array = {
						array = PIE_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = LOM_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = VNT_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = TUS_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = NAP_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = SCY_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = SAR_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = ITA
		set_country_flag = ITA_balkanize
		ITA = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = ITA_Confed
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #balkanize (merchant republic)
		name = annex.103.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = centrist
				has_government = national_conservative
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ITA
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = VNT
					is_core_of = GEN
					is_core_of = PIS
					is_core_of = AMA
				}
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_puppet_merch
		puppet = ITA
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.103.o4
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = ITA_annex
	}

country_event = { #Midwest America
	id = annex.144
	title = annex.144.t
	desc = annex.144.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = MWA
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = MWA_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = MWA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = MWA
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = MWA_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = MWA
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet (not unifier)
		name = annex.144.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MWA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			MWA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		MWA = {
			clr_country_flag = unifying_america
			clr_country_flag = can_core_ARI
			clr_country_flag = can_core_PCA
			clr_country_flag = can_core_LIN
			clr_country_flag = can_core_MOT
			clr_country_flag = can_core_TEX
			clr_country_flag = can_core_GRL
			clr_country_flag = can_core_ILL
			clr_country_flag = can_core_USA
			clr_country_flag = can_core_NEA
		}
		puppet = MWA
	}

	option = { #puppet (unifier)
		name = annex.144.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = NEA
				tag = AMC
				tag = USA
				tag = ILL
				tag = GRL
				tag = MWA
				tag = TEX
				tag = MOT
				tag = UTA
				tag = LIN
				tag = ARI
				tag = PCA
				tag = CSD
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = national_conservative
				has_government = centrist
				has_government = liberal
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { #dont make unifiers if you have American allies
				any_allied_country = {
					is_puppet = no
					OR = {
						tag = NEA
						tag = AMC
						tag = USA
						tag = ILL
						tag = GRL
						tag = TEX
						tag = MWA
						tag = MOT
						tag = UTA
						tag = LIN
						tag = ARI
						tag = PCA
						tag = CSD
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_mainland_american_state = yes
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			MWA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = MWA
		MWA = {
			set_country_flag = unifying_america
			set_country_flag = can_core_ARI
			set_country_flag = can_core_PCA
			set_country_flag = can_core_LIN
			set_country_flag = can_core_MOT
			set_country_flag = can_core_TEX
			set_country_flag = can_core_GRL
			set_country_flag = can_core_ILL
			set_country_flag = can_core_USA
			set_country_flag = can_core_NEA
		}
	}

	option = { #give to american ally/puppet
		name = annex.144.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MWA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_country = { #this should only be one possible country
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.144.o4
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = MWA_annex
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {

				is_core_of = MOT
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = LIN
				}
			}
			MOT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = MOT
	}

	option = { #give to american ally/puppet
		name = annex.147.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MOT
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_country = { #this should only be one possible country
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.147.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = MOT_annex
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}

				limit = {

						is_core_of = NEA
					}

						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = NEA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = NEA
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = NEA_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = NEA
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet (not unifier)
		name = annex.164.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_focus_tree = great_lakes_tree
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = NEA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 901
					state = 902
				}
			}
			NEA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		NEA = {
			clr_country_flag = unifying_america
			clr_country_flag = can_core_ARI
			clr_country_flag = can_core_PCA
			clr_country_flag = can_core_LIN
			clr_country_flag = can_core_MOT
			clr_country_flag = can_core_TEX
			clr_country_flag = can_core_GRL
			clr_country_flag = can_core_ILL
			clr_country_flag = can_core_USA
			clr_country_flag = can_core_MWA
		}
		puppet = NEA
		NEA = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEA_Syndicates

		}

				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {

				is_core_of = PCA

				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}

	}

			base = 0
		}

					}
				}
			}
		}

	id = annex.214
	title = annex.214.t
	desc = annex.214.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SCY 
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = SCY_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = SCY
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SCY
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = SCY_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = SCY
			}
		}
	}

			base = 100
		}

				is_core_of = SCY

					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT

			}
			SCY = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = SCY
	}

	option = { #give to ITA

		}
		trigger = {

				tag = ITA

				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SCY
				is_owned_by = ROOT

					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT

				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SOV
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = SOV_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = SOV
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = SOV
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = SOV_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = SOV
			}
		}
	}

		name = annex.227.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = the_united_states_are_back
						NOT = {
							has_government = communist
						}
					}
					tag = AMS
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SOV
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			SOV = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SOV = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
			}
		}
		puppet = SOV
	}

	option = { #balkanize
		name = annex.227.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}

		set_country_flag = SOV_balkanize
	}

			base = 0
		}

	}

country_event = { #Texas
	id = annex.245
	title = annex.245.t
	desc = annex.245.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.245.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TEX
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 894
					state = 376
				}
			}
			TEX = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = TEX
	}

	option = { #give to USA
		name = annex.245.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = USA
			}
			USA = {
				exists = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TEX
				NOT = {
					state = 894
					state = 376
				}
			}
			USA = {
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TEX
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 894
					state = 376
				}
			}
			USA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to american ally/puppet
		name = annex.245.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TEX
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_country = { #this should only be one possible country
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #annex
		name = annex.245.o4
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = TEX_annex
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #USA (American Republic)
	id = annex.263
	title = annex.263.t
	desc = annex.263.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = USA
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = USA_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = USA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = USA
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = USA_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = USA
			}
			USA = {
				clr_country_flag = robert_bentley_elected
				clr_country_flag = donald_rumsfeld_elected
				clr_country_flag = jeb_bush_elected
				clr_country_flag = david_duke_elected
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet (not unifier)
		name = annex.263.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_focus_tree = great_lakes_tree
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 901
					state = 902
				}
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = PUE
				}
			}
			USA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		USA = {
			clr_country_flag = unifying_america
			clr_country_flag = can_core_ARI
			clr_country_flag = can_core_PCA
			clr_country_flag = can_core_LIN
			clr_country_flag = can_core_MOT
			clr_country_flag = can_core_TEX
			clr_country_flag = can_core_GRL
			clr_country_flag = can_core_ILL
			clr_country_flag = can_core_NEA
			clr_country_flag = can_core_MWA
		}
		USA = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CSA
		}
		puppet = USA
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = USA_joseph_votel
							ruling_only = no
						}
					}
					retire_character = USA_joseph_votel
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet (unifier)
		name = annex.263.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = NEA
				tag = AMC
				tag = USA
				tag = ILL
				tag = GRL
				tag = MWA
				tag = TEX
				tag = MOT
				tag = UTA
				tag = LIN
				tag = ARI
				tag = PCA
				tag = CSD
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = fascist
				has_government = nationalist
				has_government = monarchist
				has_government = national_conservative
				has_government = liberal
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
			NOT = { #dont make unifiers if you have American allies
				any_allied_country = {
					is_puppet = no
					OR = {
						tag = NEA
						tag = AMC
						tag = USA
						tag = ILL
						tag = GRL
						tag = TEX
						tag = MWA
						tag = MOT
						tag = UTA
						tag = LIN
						tag = ARI
						tag = PCA
						tag = CSD
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_mainland_american_state = yes
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					owner = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			USA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		USA = {
			set_country_flag = unifying_america
			set_country_flag = can_core_ARI
			set_country_flag = can_core_PCA
			set_country_flag = can_core_LIN
			set_country_flag = can_core_MOT
			set_country_flag = can_core_TEX
			set_country_flag = can_core_GRL
			set_country_flag = can_core_ILL
			set_country_flag = can_core_NEA
			set_country_flag = can_core_MWA
		}
		USA = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		}
		puppet = USA
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = USA_joseph_votel
							ruling_only = no
						}
					}
					retire_character = USA_joseph_votel
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascist
			}
			country_event = annex.296
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = nationalist
			}
			country_event = annex.297
		}
	}

	option = { #give to american ally/puppet
		name = annex.263.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_focus_tree = great_lakes_tree
			}
			any_country = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = USA
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_country = { #this should only be one possible country
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = {#special GRL option

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			has_focus_tree = great_lakes_tree
		}
		country_event = greatlakes_diplo.16
	}

	option = { #annex

			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = USA_annex
		trigger = {

country_event = { #Venice
	id = annex.269
	title = annex.269.t
	desc = annex.269.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = VNT
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = VNT_starting_cores
						value = THIS
					}
				}
				add_core_of = VNT
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = VNT
					NOT = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = VNT_starting_cores
							value = THIS
						}
					}
				}
				remove_core_of = VNT
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.269.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = VNT
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			VNT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = VNT
	}

	option = { #give to ITA
		name = annex.269.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = ITA
			}
			ITA = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet_of = ROOT

				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = VNT
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT

			ITA = {

country_event = { #East Cascadia
	id = annex.310
	title = annex.310.t
	desc = annex.310.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #give to CSD
		name = annex.310.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = CSD
			}
			CSD = {
				exists = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		890 = {
			CSD = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to LIN

		}

				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to MOT

			base = 100
		}

				exists = yes

					AND = {

							is_puppet_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT

						has_country_flag = unifying_america
					}
				}
			}
		}
		890 = {
			MOT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to american ally/puppet

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
			}
		}
		890 = {
			every_country = { #this should only be one possible country
				limit = {

						is_puppet_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
					has_country_flag = unifying_america
				}
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #annex

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}

		set_country_flag = east_csd_annex

							is_in_faction_with = ROOT

					}
				}
			}
